NB: The 'Reason' is an abbreviation, check any referenced bugs for more
    details.

Keys:

  o ROM == Request Of Maintainer
  o RoQA == Requested by the QA team
  o ROP == Request of Porter
  o ROSRM == Request of Stable Release Manager
  o NBS == Not Built [by] Source
  o NPOASR == Never Part Of A Stable Release
  o NVIU == Newer Version In Unstable (for experimental removals)
  o NVIT == Newer Version In Testing (for testing-proposed-updates removals)
  o ANAIS == Architecture Not Allowed In Source
  o ICE == Internal Compiler Error
  o [rene] == detected by the cruft finder script 'rene'
